<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多孤立评估LLM在自动作文评分中的单一技术，缺乏对不同方法在英语二语写作场景下综合性能的系统比较，限制了对技术优劣的理解与应用。

Method: 在统一的IELTS Writing Task 2基准上，系统评估四类LLM-based AES方法：(i) 编码器分类微调；(ii) 零/少样本提示；(iii) 指令微调+RAG；(iv) 监督微调+DPO+RAG。通过标准化实验设置，量化各方法在准确性、成本与鲁棒性上的表现。

Result: 不同方法呈现清晰的准确率-成本-鲁棒性权衡；最优配置（k-SFT + RAG）达到93% F1-score，显著优于其他方法；验证了RAG在提升评分一致性与上下文理解方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了首个针对英语二语写作的现代LLM-AES策略的统一比较，揭示了各方法的适用边界与协同潜力，为自动评分系统的开发与部署提供了实证指导。代码已开源，支持可复现性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have recently reshaped Automated Essay Scoring (AES), yet prior studies typically examine individual techniques in isolation, limiting understanding of their relative merits for English as a Second Language (L2) writing. To bridge this gap, we presents a comprehensive comparison of major LLM-based AES paradigms on IELTS Writing Task~2. On this unified benchmark, we evaluate four approaches: (i) encoder-based classification fine-tuning, (ii) zero- and few-shot prompting, (iii) instruction tuning and Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), and (iv) Supervised Fine-Tuning combined with Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) and RAG. Our results reveal clear accuracy-cost-robustness trade-offs across methods, the best configuration, integrating k-SFT and RAG, achieves the strongest overall results with F1-Score 93%. This study offers the first unified empirical comparison of modern LLM-based AES strategies for English L2, promising potential in auto-grading writing tasks. Code is public at https://github.com/MinhNguyenDS/LLM_AES-EnL2

### [161] [Abductive Reasoning with Syllogistic Forms in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06428)
*Hirohiko Abe,Risako Ando,Takanobu Morishita Kentaro Ozeki,Koji Mineshima,Mitsuhiro Okada*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLMs）在类比推理中的准确性，通过将传统三段论数据集转换为适合类比推理的形式，旨在评估最先进的LLMs在类比推理中是否存在偏差，并识别改进方向。研究强调了超越形式演绎的语境化推理的重要性，对推动LLMs在复杂推理任务中的应用具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究发现LLMs与人类在推理中存在相似的偏见，例如忽视与常识相悖但逻辑有效的推论。然而，这种批评可能不公平，因为人类推理不仅包括形式演绎，还包括基于有限信息进行初步推断的类比推理。因此，有必要考察LLMs在类比推理中的表现，以更全面地理解其认知能力。

Method: 将传统的三段论数据集转换为适用于类比推理的任务格式，用于评估当前最先进的大语言模型在类比推理中的表现。

Result: 研究发现，尽管LLMs在形式推理中表现出色，但在类比推理任务中仍存在显著偏差，尤其在处理与常识冲突的情境时表现不佳。这表明现有模型在语境化推理方面仍有改进空间。

Conclusion: LLMs在类比推理中存在系统性偏差，提示需要发展更具情境敏感性的推理机制。未来的研究应聚焦于增强模型的语境理解与非形式化推理能力，以缩小机器与人类认知之间的差距。

Abstract: Research in AI using Large-Language Models (LLMs) is rapidly evolving, and the comparison of their performance with human reasoning has become a key concern. Prior studies have indicated that LLMs and humans share similar biases, such as dismissing logically valid inferences that contradict common beliefs. However, criticizing LLMs for these biases might be unfair, considering our reasoning not only involves formal deduction but also abduction, which draws tentative conclusions from limited information. Abduction can be regarded as the inverse form of syllogism in its basic structure, that is, a process of drawing a minor premise from a major premise and conclusion. This paper explores the accuracy of LLMs in abductive reasoning by converting a syllogistic dataset into one suitable for abduction. It aims to investigate whether the state-of-the-art LLMs exhibit biases in abduction and to identify potential areas for improvement, emphasizing the importance of contextualized reasoning beyond formal deduction. This investigation is vital for advancing the understanding and application of LLMs in complex reasoning tasks, offering insights into bridging the gap between machine and human cognition.

### [162] [PONTE: Personalized Orchestration for Natural Language Trustworthy Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06485)
*Vittoria Vineis,Matteo Silvestri,Lorenzo Antonelli,Filippo Betello,Gabriele Tolomei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PONTE 是一种以人为本的自适应可解释人工智能（XAI）框架，通过闭环验证与适应机制实现个性化、可信的自然语言解释。它结合低维偏好模型、基于结构化XAI成果的条件生成器以及验证模块，确保解释的忠实性、完整性和风格一致性，并通过用户反馈迭代优化偏好状态。在医疗和金融领域的人工与自动评估中，该方法显著提升了解释的完整性与风格契合度，且人类研究证实其能有效匹配用户意图，具备鲁棒性和高质量评价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有XAI方法多采用‘一刀切’模式，忽视用户在专业知识、目标和认知需求上的差异；尽管大语言模型可将技术解释转化为自然语言，但存在忠实度不足和幻觉问题，亟需更可靠、个性化的解释生成机制。

Method: PONTE采用闭环验证与适应机制，包含：(i) 低维偏好模型捕捉用户风格偏好；(ii) 偏好条件生成器基于结构化XAI结果生成解释；(iii) 验证模块确保数值忠实性、信息完整性和风格一致性，支持检索增强论证。用户反馈用于动态更新偏好状态，实现快速个性化。

Result: 在医疗和金融领域的自动与人工评估中，带有验证-精炼循环的PONTE显著优于无验证的生成方式，在信息完整性和风格一致性方面表现更优；人类研究表明，系统能准确反映用户预期偏好，对生成随机性具有鲁棒性，且整体解释质量获得一致认可。

Conclusion: PONTE通过构建人机协同的闭环个性化机制，实现了高可信度、自适应的自然语言解释，为复杂场景下的可解释人工智能提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Explainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI) seeks to enhance the transparency and accountability of machine learning systems, yet most methods follow a one-size-fits-all paradigm that neglects user differences in expertise, goals, and cognitive needs. Although Large Language Models can translate technical explanations into natural language, they introduce challenges related to faithfulness and hallucinations. To address these challenges, we present PONTE (Personalized Orchestration for Natural language Trustworthy Explanations), a human-in-the-loop framework for adaptive and reliable XAI narratives. PONTE models personalization as a closed-loop validation and adaptation process rather than prompt engineering. It combines: (i) a low-dimensional preference model capturing stylistic requirements; (ii) a preference-conditioned generator grounded in structured XAI artifacts; and (iii) verification modules enforcing numerical faithfulness, informational completeness, and stylistic alignment, optionally supported by retrieval-grounded argumentation. User feedback iteratively updates the preference state, enabling quick personalization. Automatic and human evaluations across healthcare and finance domains show that the verification-refinement loop substantially improves completeness and stylistic alignment over validation-free generation. Human studies further confirm strong agreement between intended preference vectors and perceived style, robustness to generation stochasticity, and consistently positive quality assessments.

</details>


### [163] [Speak in Context: Multilingual ASR with Speech Context Alignment via Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06505)
*Yuchen Zhang,Haralambos Mouratidis,Ravi Shekhar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种支持多语言和多种口音的上下文感知语音识别框架，通过轻量级投影模块结合冻结的语音编码器与仅解码器的语言模型，实现对对话历史和偏置词等结构化上下文提示的引导。采用对比学习目标在共享嵌入空间中对齐语音与上下文表示，显著提升跨模态交互效果。在覆盖11种语言和5种英语方言的超过1500小时真实对话语音上评估，上下文输入持续提升识别质量，对比对齐带来额外超过5%的整体性能增益，验证了上下文建模与跨模态对齐的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动语音识别系统大多局限于单语环境和短孤立语音，尽管上下文感知ASR有进展，但仍面临多语言支持有限和语音与上下文表示缺乏合理对齐两大挑战。

Method: 结合冻结的语音编码器与解码器-only语言模型，通过轻量级投影模块实现结构化上下文提示（如对话历史、偏置词）的引导；引入对比学习目标，在共享嵌入空间中对齐语音与上下文表示，增强跨模态交互。

Result: 在超过1500小时的真实对话语音数据（11种语言，5种英语方言）上，上下文输入持续提升识别准确率；对比对齐在不同上下文类型下进一步带来性能增益，整体提升超过5%。

Conclusion: 上下文建模与跨模态对齐在多语言自动语音识别中至关重要，所提框架有效提升了多语言、多口音场景下的语音识别性能，且保持了预训练模型的模块化优势。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition (ASR) has benefited from advances in pretrained speech and language models, yet most systems remain constrained to monolingual settings and short, isolated utterances. While recent efforts in context-aware ASR show promise, two key challenges persist: limited multilingual support and the absence of principled alignment between speech and contextual representations. In this paper, we introduce a context-aware multilingual ASR framework that supports diverse languages and accents while preserving the modularity of pretrained models. Our approach combines a frozen speech encoder and a decoder-only language model via a lightweight projection module, allowing structured context prompts, including dialogue history and biasing words, to guide transcription. To improve interaction between speech and context, we employ a contrastive learning objective that aligns their representations in a shared embedding space. Evaluations on over 1,500 hours of real-world conversational speech across 11 languages and 5 English dialects show that contextual input consistently improves recognition quality. Contrastive alignment provides additional gains when applied to different context types, with an overall performance gain of over 5%. These results highlight the importance of both contextual modeling and cross-modal alignment in multilingual ASR.

</details>


### [164] [KCLarity at SemEval-2026 Task 6: Encoder and Zero-Shot Approaches to Political Evasion Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06552)
*Archie Sage,Salvatore Greco*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: KCLarity团队参与SemEval 2026的CLARITY共享任务，研究两种建模方法：直接预测清晰度标签，或先预测规避标签并基于任务分类层级推导清晰度。还探索了多种辅助训练策略，并在零样本设置下评估解码器仅模型。两种方法表现相当；RoBERTa-large在公开测试集上表现最佳，而零样本GPT-5.2在隐藏评估集上泛化能力更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在提升政治话语中模糊性与规避技巧的自动识别能力，通过不同建模范式探索更有效的分类方法。

Method: 采用两种建模方式：直接预测清晰度标签，或先预测规避标签再通过分类层级推导清晰度；结合辅助训练策略，使用编码器和解码器仅模型进行实验，包含零样本设置下的评估。

Result: 两种建模方法性能相近；RoBERTa-large在公开测试集上表现最优，零样本GPT-5.2在隐藏评估集上泛化能力更优。

Conclusion: 两种建模范式均有效，具体模型选择需根据数据集特性及评估目标权衡，零样本模型在未见数据上展现出良好泛化潜力。

Abstract: This paper describes the KCLarity team's participation in CLARITY, a shared task at SemEval 2026 on classifying ambiguity and evasion techniques in political discourse. We investigate two modelling formulations: (i) directly predicting the clarity label, and (ii) predicting the evasion label and deriving clarity through the task taxonomy hierarchy. We further explore several auxiliary training variants and evaluate decoder-only models in a zero-shot setting under the evasion-first formulation. Overall, the two formulations yield comparable performance. Among encoder-based models, RoBERTa-large achieves the strongest results on the public test set, while zero-shot GPT-5.2 generalises better on the hidden evaluation set.

### [165] [RoboLayout: Differentiable 3D Scene Generation for Embodied Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05522)
*Ali Shamsaddinlou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RoboLayout extends LayoutVLM by integrating agent-aware reasoning and reachability constraints for generating feasible, interactive 3D indoor layouts. It supports diverse agents (robots, humans, animals) and includes a local refinement stage to improve optimization efficiency.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing vision-language models struggle to generate physically plausible and interaction-friendly indoor layouts, especially in constrained environments. There is a need for agent-centric design that ensures navigability and actionability for embodied agents.

Method: RoboLayout enhances LayoutVLM with differentiable reachability constraints and a local refinement stage. It models agent capabilities abstractly, enabling flexible environment design across various agent types while improving optimization stability and convergence.

Result: Experiments show RoboLayout maintains strong semantic alignment and physical plausibility while significantly improving layout feasibility for embodied agents across diverse scene configurations.

Conclusion: RoboLayout advances agent-centric indoor scene generation by enabling physically realistic, navigable, and actionable layouts through integrated reachability modeling and efficient optimization, applicable to a wide range of agent types.

Abstract: Recent advances in vision language models (VLMs) have shown strong potential for spatial reasoning and 3D scene layout generation from open-ended language instructions. However, generating layouts that are not only semantically coherent but also feasible for interaction by embodied agents remains challenging, particularly in physically constrained indoor environments. In this paper, RoboLayout is introduced as an extension of LayoutVLM that augments the original framework with agent-aware reasoning and improved optimization stability. RoboLayout integrates explicit reachability constraints into a differentiable layout optimization process, enabling the generation of layouts that are navigable and actionable by embodied agents. Importantly, the agent abstraction is not limited to a specific robot platform and can represent diverse entities with distinct physical capabilities, such as service robots, warehouse robots, humans of different age groups, or animals, allowing environment design to be tailored to the intended agent. In addition, a local refinement stage is proposed that selectively reoptimizes problematic object placements while keeping the remainder of the scene fixed, improving convergence efficiency without increasing global optimization iterations. Overall, RoboLayout preserves the strong semantic alignment and physical plausibility of LayoutVLM while enhancing applicability to agent-centric indoor scene generation, as demonstrated by experimental results across diverse scene configurations.

</details>


### [166] [Reasoning Models Struggle to Control their Chains of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05706)
*Chen Yueh-Han,Robert McCarthy,Bruce W. Lee,He He,Ian Kivlichan,Bowen Baker,Micah Carroll,Tomek Korbak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CoT-Control评估套件，用于衡量模型在遵循思维链（CoT）指令时控制其输出的能力。研究发现，推理模型的CoT可控性远低于输出可控性，例如Claude Sonnet 4.5在CoT中仅2.7%时间能控制输出，而在最终输出中可达61.9%。大模型、强化学习训练、测试时计算量和问题难度对可控性有显著影响。即使在激励下，模型仍难以规避监控，且对抗性提示也未明显提升可控性。尽管如此，当前仍对CoT监控能力保持谨慎乐观，但其背后机制尚不明确，建议前沿实验室持续追踪此指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检测现代推理模型中可能存在的恶意行为并理解其动机，需依赖思维链（CoT）监控。若模型能操控其在CoT中的表述，则会削弱监控有效性，因此亟需评估模型对CoT的可控程度。

Method: 构建CoT-Control评估套件，设计需在遵守特定限制条件下完成推理任务的测试场景（如避免使用'染色体'一词），通过实验测量不同模型在多种条件下的CoT可控性表现，并分析规模、训练方式、计算资源及任务难度的影响。

Result: 推理模型的CoT可控性显著低于输出可控性；大模型表现出更高可控性，而更多强化学习训练、更大测试时计算量和更难的问题会降低可控性；即使存在激励或对抗性提示，可控性提升有限；模型在被告知被监控时略有提高。

Conclusion: 当前CoT可控性尚未构成对CoT监控能力的主要威胁，但其内在机制仍不清楚，建议未来对前沿模型持续监测该指标。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is a promising tool for detecting misbehaviors and understanding the motivations of modern reasoning models. However, if models can control what they verbalize in their CoT, it could undermine CoT monitorability. To measure this undesirable capability -- CoT controllability -- we introduce the CoT-Control evaluation suite, which includes tasks that require models to solve problems while adhering to CoT instructions, e.g., reasoning about a genetics question without using the word 'chromosome'. We show that reasoning models possess significantly lower CoT controllability than output controllability; for instance, Claude Sonnet 4.5 can control its CoT only 2.7% of the time but 61.9% when controlling its final output. We also find that CoT controllability is higher for larger models and decreases with more RL training, test-time compute, and increased problem difficulty. CoT controllability failures extend even to situations in which models are given incentives (as opposed to direct requests) to evade CoT monitors, although models exhibit slightly higher controllability when they are told they are being monitored. Similarly, eliciting controllability by adversarially optimizing prompts does not meaningfully increase controllability. Our results leave us cautiously optimistic that CoT controllability is currently unlikely to be a failure mode of CoT monitorability. However, the mechanism behind low controllability is not well understood. Given its importance for maintaining CoT monitorability, we recommend that frontier labs track CoT controllability in future models.

</details>


### [167] [The World Won't Stay Still: Programmable Evolution for Agent Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05910)
*Guangrui Li,Yaochen Xie,Yi Liu,Ziwei Dong,Xingyuan Pan,Tianqi Zheng,Jason Choi,Michael J. Morais,Binit Jha,Shaunak Mishra,Bingrou Zhou,Chen Luo,Monica Xiao Cheng,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ProEvolve，一个基于图的框架，用于可编程地演化智能体环境。通过类型化的关系图统一表示数据、工具和模式，实现对环境演化的可控与可扩展。该框架支持通过图变换自动生成多样化环境与任务沙箱，并在200个环境和3,000个沙箱上验证了其有效性，以更真实地评估智能体的适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试多假设静态环境，忽略现实世界中环境随时间演化的动态性，导致难以评估智能体在变化环境中的鲁棒性和适应能力。因此需要一种可控制、可扩展的环境演化机制来更真实地评估智能体性能。

Method: 提出基于类型化关系图的统一表示形式，将环境中的数据、工具和模式结构化；通过图变换实现环境的增删改操作，并保证更新在工具、模式和数据访问间一致传播；利用子图采样与编程生成多样化的任务沙箱，支持自动化环境演化。

Result: 成功从单一环境演化出200个不同环境和3,000个任务沙箱，并在这些环境中对代表性智能体进行基准测试，验证了框架的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: ProEvolve提供了一种高效、可控且可扩展的环境演化方法，能够显著提升对智能体适应能力的评估真实性，为未来动态环境下的智能体研究提供了重要基础。

Abstract: LLM-powered agents fulfill user requests by interacting with environments, querying data, and invoking tools in a multi-turn process. Yet, most existing benchmarks assume static environments with fixed schemas and toolsets, neglecting the evolutionary nature of the real world and agents' robustness to environmental changes. In this paper, we study a crucial problem: how to evolve the agent environment in a scalable and controllable way, thereby better evaluating agents' adaptability to real-world dynamics. We propose ProEvolve, a graph-based framework that makes environment evolution programmable. At its core, a typed relational graph provides a unified, explicit representation of the environment: data, tools, and schema. Under this formalism, adding, removing, or modifying capabilities are expressed as graph transformations that coherently propagate updates across tools, schemas, and data access. Building on this, ProEvolve can (1) program the evolutionary dynamics as graph transformations to generate environments automatically, and (2) instantiate task sandboxes via subgraph sampling and programming. We validate ProEvolve by evolving a single environment into 200 environments and 3,000 task sandboxes, and benchmark representative agents accordingly.

</details>


### [168] [DeepFact: Co-Evolving Benchmarks and Agents for Deep Research Factuality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05912)
*Yukun Huang,Leonardo F. R. Ribeiro,Momchil Hardalov,Bhuwan Dhingra,Markus Dreyer,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出AtS（Audit-then-Score）方法，通过可修订的基准测试提升深度研究报告（DRR）中事实性验证的可靠性。在四轮迭代后，专家标注准确率从60.8%提升至90.9%，并构建了DeepFact-Bench和DeepFact-Eval，显著优于现有验证器且具备良好泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事实核查工具主要针对通用领域、原子性事实声明，难以有效评估深度研究报告中的复杂主张；而构建可靠基准本身困难，尤其因专家单次标注易出错，需一种动态可修正的验证机制。

Method: 提出Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score（AtS）：当验证器与基准标签冲突时，需提交证据，由专家审计员裁决，采纳合理修改以更新基准，形成闭环迭代。

Result: 在四轮AtS迭代中，专家在微黄金数据集上的准确率从60.8%提升至90.9%；基于AtS构建的DeepFact-Bench具有可审计的推理链，DeepFact-Eval在该基准上表现优异，并在外部数据集上展现出良好迁移能力。

Conclusion: AtS机制能显著提升深度研究报告事实性评估的准确性与可信度，所提出的DeepFact-Bench与DeepFact-Eval为高阶事实核查提供了有效工具与基准支持。

Abstract: Search-augmented LLM agents can produce deep research reports (DRRs), but verifying claim-level factuality remains challenging. Existing fact-checkers are primarily designed for general-domain, factoid-style atomic claims, and there is no benchmark to test whether such verifiers transfer to DRRs. Yet building such a benchmark is itself difficult. We first show that static expert-labeled benchmarks are brittle in this setting: in a controlled study with PhD-level specialists, unassisted experts achieve only 60.8% accuracy on a hidden micro-gold set of verifiable claims. We propose Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS), where benchmark labels and rationales are explicitly revisable: when a verifier disagrees with the current benchmark, it must submit evidence; an auditor adjudicates the dispute; and accepted revisions update the benchmark before models are scored. Across four AtS rounds, expert micro-gold accuracy rises to 90.9%, indicating experts are substantially more reliable as auditors than as one-shot labelers. We instantiate AtS as DeepFact-Bench, a versioned DRR factuality benchmark with auditable rationales, and DeepFact-Eval, a document-level verification agent (with a grouped lite variant) that outperforms existing verifiers on DeepFact-Bench and transfers well to external factuality datasets.

</details>

Abstract: Product concept evaluation is a critical stage that determines strategic resource allocation and project success in enterprises. However, traditional expert-led approaches face limitations such as subjective bias and high time and cost requirements. To support this process, this study proposes an automated approach utilizing a large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent system (MAS). Through a systematic analysis of previous research on product development and team collaboration, this study established two primary evaluation dimensions, namely technical feasibility and market feasibility. The proposed system consists of a team of eight virtual agents representing specialized domains such as R&D and marketing. These agents use retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and real-time search tools to gather objective evidence and validate concepts through structured deliberations based on the established criteria. The agents were further fine-tuned using professional product review data to enhance their judgment accuracy. These results confirm the usability of the proposed multi-agent-based evaluation approach for supporting product development decisions.

### [170] [Aggregative Semantics for Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06067)
*Yann Munro,Isabelle Bloch,Marie-Jeanne Lesot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的渐进语义家族——聚合语义，用于定量双极论证框架（QBAF），该框架中论证具有内在权重，并可相互攻击或支持。与传统模块化语义不同，该方法分别聚合攻击者和支持者的贡献，再与论证的内在权重结合，形成三阶段计算过程。这种方法增强了对双极性的建模能力，提升了语义的可解释性与参数化灵活性，并通过实例验证了其在多种情境下的行为表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有渐进语义在处理攻击与支持角色不对称时存在局限，且难以保持双极性信息的清晰表达。因此需要一种更具解释性和灵活性的语义框架来更准确地反映论证之间的复杂关系。

Method: 提出三阶段聚合机制：首先分别计算攻击者和支持者的全局权重，然后将这两个值与论证的内在权重进行聚合，使用三个可配置的聚合函数实现灵活建模。

Result: 实验表明，在500种不同聚合语义组合下，该方法展现出丰富的行为模式；所提语义满足经典渐进语义原则，并在可解释性与参数化方面优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 聚合语义提供了一种更灵活、可解释性更强的渐进语义框架，能够有效处理攻击与支持的非对称性，扩展了定量双极论证框架的建模能力。

Abstract: Formal argumentation is being used increasingly in artificial intelligence as an effective and understandable way to model potentially conflicting pieces of information, called arguments, and identify so-called acceptable arguments depending on a chosen semantics. This paper deals with the specific context of Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks (QBAF), where arguments have intrinsic weights and can attack or support each other. In this context, we introduce a novel family of gradual semantics, called aggregative semantics. In order to deal with situations in which attackers and supporters do not play a symmetric role, and in contrast to modular semantics, we propose to aggregate attackers and supporters separately. This leads to a three-stage computation, which consists in computing a global weight for attackers and another for supporters, before aggregating these two values with the intrinsic weight of the argument. We discuss the properties that the three aggregation functions should satisfy depending on the context, as well as their relationships with the classical principles for gradual semantics. This discussion is supported by various simple examples, as well as a final example on which five hundred aggregative semantics are tested and compared, illustrating the range of possible behaviours with aggregative semantics. Decomposing the computation into three distinct and interpretable steps leads to a more parametrisable computation: it keeps the bipolarity one step further than what is done in the literature, and it leads to more understandable gradual semantics.

</details>

Method: 提出CliqueFlowmer，融合团基模型基于优化（clique-based MBO）与Transformer及流生成模型，实现对目标材料属性的直接优化生成。

Abstract: Recent advances in deep learning inspired neural network-based approaches to computational materials discovery (CMD). A plethora of problems in this field involve finding materials that optimize a target property. Nevertheless, the increasingly popular generative modeling methods are ineffective at boldly exploring attractive regions of the materials space due to their maximum likelihood training. In this work, we offer an alternative CMD technique based on offline model-based optimization (MBO) that fuses direct optimization of a target material property into generation. To that end, we introduce a domain-specific model, dubbed CliqueFlowmer, that incorporates recent advances of clique-based MBO into transformer and flow generation. We validate CliqueFlowmer's optimization abilities and show that materials it produces strongly outperform those provided by generative baselines. In this work, we propose a novel decision-support framework using reinforcement learning (RL) for long-term flood adaptation planning. Formulated as an integrated assessment model (IAM), the framework combines rainfall projection and flood modeling, transport simulation, and quantification of direct and indirect impacts on infrastructure and mobility. Our RL-based approach learns adaptive strategies that balance investment and maintenance costs against avoided impacts. We evaluate the framework through a case study of Copenhagen's inner city over the 2024-2100 period, testing multiple adaptation options, and different belief and realized climate scenarios. Results show that the framework outperforms traditional optimization approaches by discovering coordinated spatial and temporal adaptation pathways and learning trade-offs between impact reduction and adaptation investment, yielding more resilient strategies. Overall, our results showcase the potential of reinforcement learning as a flexible decision-support tool for adaptive infrastructure planning under climate uncertainty.

### [173] [SAHOO: Safeguarded Alignment for High-Order Optimization Objectives in Recursive Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06333)
*Subramanyam Sahoo,Aman Chadha,Vinija Jain,Divya Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SAHOO 是一个用于监控和控制递归自我改进中对齐漂移的实用框架，包含三个防护机制：目标漂移指数（GDI）、约束保持检查和回归风险量化。在189个任务中，该框架在代码生成和推理任务上分别实现了18.3%和16.8%的质量提升，同时在两个领域保持了约束，并在真实性方面维持低违规率。阈值通过小规模验证集校准，研究还揭示了能力-对齐前沿的动态变化，表明早期改进高效但后期对齐成本上升，且存在领域特异性张力（如流畅性与事实性）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代系统已具备自我批评、修改和评估输出的能力，但迭代自修改可能引发微妙的对齐漂移，威胁系统安全与可靠性，亟需可测量、可部署、可验证的对齐监控机制。

Method: 提出SAHOO框架，采用多信号融合的学习除了目标漂移指数（GDI），结合语义、词汇、结构和分布度量；引入约束保持检查以确保语法正确性和非幻觉；并通过回归风险量化识别可能抵消先前改进的优化周期。

Result: 在189项任务中，代码生成任务提升18.3%，数学推理任务提升16.8%；在两个领域成功保持约束，真实性任务中违规率低；阈值基于18个任务的小规模验证集校准，有效揭示能力与对齐之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: SAHOO使递归自我改进过程中的对齐保持变得可测量、可部署、可系统验证，为大规模应用提供了可靠保障。

Abstract: Recursive self-improvement is moving from theory to practice: modern systems can critique, revise, and evaluate their own outputs, yet iterative self-modification risks subtle alignment drift. We introduce SAHOO, a practical framework to monitor and control drift through three safeguards: (i) the Goal Drift Index (GDI), a learned multi-signal detector combining semantic, lexical, structural, and distributional measures; (ii) constraint preservation checks that enforce safety-critical invariants such as syntactic correctness and non-hallucination; and (iii) regression-risk quantification to flag improvement cycles that undo prior gains. Across 189 tasks in code generation, mathematical reasoning, and truthfulness, SAHOO produces substantial quality gains, including 18.3 percent improvement in code tasks and 16.8 percent in reasoning, while preserving constraints in two domains and maintaining low violations in truthfulness. Thresholds are calibrated on a small validation set of 18 tasks across three cycles. We further map the capability-alignment frontier, showing efficient early improvement cycles but rising alignment costs later and exposing domain-specific tensions such as fluency versus factuality. SAHOO therefore makes alignment preservation during recursive self-improvement measurable, deployable, and systematically validated at scale.

</details>


### [174] [Talk Freely, Execute Strictly: Schema-Gated Agentic AI for Flexible and Reproducible Scientific Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06394)
*Joel Strickland,Arjun Vijeta,Chris Moores,Oliwia Bodek,Bogdan Nenchev,Thomas Whitehead,Charles Phillips,Karl Tassenberg,Gareth Conduit,Ben Pellegrini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出以模式约束编排（schema-gated orchestration）解决大语言模型在科学工作流中既需确定性又需对话灵活性的矛盾。通过20个系统的评估，发现高灵活性与高确定性难以兼得，但存在一个收敛区域。研究提出三原则：执行前澄清、受控规划-执行编排、工具到工作流层级的约束，以实现解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学工作流需要确定性、可追溯性和治理能力，而大语言模型在生成计算时难以保证这些特性。现有系统在对话灵活性与执行确定性之间存在冲突，亟需一种既能保持灵活性又能确保安全可控的架构方案。

Method: 采用半结构化访谈收集18位工业研发专家的需求；构建执行确定性（ED）与对话灵活性（CF）两个维度，对20个系统进行跨架构组评估；使用多模型协议（15次独立会话，3种LLM家族）进行评分，验证评分一致性。

Result: 评估显示各系统在灵活性与确定性间呈权衡关系，存在经验帕累托前沿；多模型评分具高度一致性（ED: Krippendorff a=0.80, CF: a=0.98），证明其可替代人工专家评审；提出模式约束架构可有效解耦矛盾，并提炼出三项操作原则。

Conclusion: 模式约束编排是一种可行的架构范式，通过分离对话与执行权限，可在不牺牲灵活性的前提下保障工作流的确定性与透明性，为科学计算自动化提供可靠路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can now translate a researcher's plain-language goal into executable computation, yet scientific workflows demand determinism, provenance, and governance that are difficult to guarantee when an LLM decides what runs. Semi-structured interviews with 18 experts across 10 industrial R&D stakeholders surface 2 competing requirements--deterministic, constrained execution and conversational flexibility without workflow rigidity--together with boundary properties (human-in-the-loop control and transparency) that any resolution must satisfy. We propose schema-gated orchestration as the resolving principle: the schema becomes a mandatory execution boundary at the composed-workflow level, so that nothing runs unless the complete action--including cross-step dependencies--validates against a machine-checkable specification.
  We operationalize the 2 requirements as execution determinism (ED) and conversational flexibility (CF), and use these axes to review 20 systems spanning 5 architectural groups along a validation-scope spectrum. Scores are assigned via a multi-model protocol--15 independent sessions across 3 LLM families--yielding substantial-to-near-perfect inter-model agreement (Krippendorff a=0.80 for ED and a=0.98 for CF), demonstrating that multi-model LLM scoring can serve as a reusable alternative to human expert panels for architectural assessment.
  The resulting landscape reveals an empirical Pareto front--no reviewed system achieves both high flexibility and high determinism--but a convergence zone emerges between the generative and workflow-centric extremes. We argue that a schema-gated architecture, separating conversational from execution authority, is positioned to decouple this trade-off, and distill 3 operational principles--clarification-before-execution, constrained plan-act orchestration, and tool-to-workflow-level gating--to guide adoption.

</details>

### [175] [VDCook:DIY video data cook your MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05539)
*Chengwei Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VDCook是一个自演化的视频数据操作系统，允许用户通过自然语言查询和参数调整来请求视频数据，系统自动执行查询优化，并行运行真实视频检索与受控合成模块，生成带有完整溯源信息和元数据的领域内数据包及可复现的Notebooks。该平台支持持续更新和领域扩展，基于MCP（模型上下文协议）实现动态演化，提供多维度元数据标注，降低构建专业视频训练数据集的门槛，促进社区贡献和治理驱动的数据扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视频数据集多为静态、一次性构建，难以满足动态变化的领域需求，且构建过程复杂、门槛高。为降低专业视频数据集构建难度，提升数据的可扩展性与可追溯性，亟需一种自动化、可配置、可持续演进的数据构建平台。

Method: 采用自然语言查询接口与可调节参数（如规模、检索-合成比例、质量阈值），结合查询优化技术，协同运行真实视频检索与可控合成模块；利用MCP（Model Context Protocol）实现自动化数据摄入，支持数据持续更新；通过多维度元数据标注（如场景分割、运动评分、OCR比例、自动字幕等）增强数据可索引性与可操作性；最终输出包含完整溯源与元数据的数据包及可复现的Notebooks。

Result: 成功构建了一个支持自然语言交互、自动优化、并行检索与合成的视频数据构造平台，实现了数据集的动态演化与可扩展性，显著降低了专业视频数据构建的技术门槛，支持社区贡献与治理机制，为后续数据‘烹饪’与索引提供了灵活基础。

Conclusion: VDCook通过基础设施级创新，将视频数据集从静态资源转变为动态、可演化的开放生态系统，为研究者与垂直领域团队提供了高效、可复现、可扩展的视频数据构建解决方案，推动了视频数据生态的可持续发展。

Abstract: We introduce VDCook: a self-evolving video data operating system, a configurable video data construction platform for researchers and vertical domain teams. Users initiate data requests via natural language queries and adjustable parameters (scale, retrieval-synthesis ratio, quality threshold). The system automatically performs query optimization, concurrently running real video retrieval and controlled synthesis modules. It ultimately generates in-domain data packages with complete provenance and metadata, along with reproducible Notebooks.
  Unlike traditional static, one-time-built datasets, VDCook enables continuous updates and domain expansion through its automated data ingestion mechanism based on MCP (Model Context Protocol)\cite{mcp2024anthropic}, transforming datasets into dynamically evolving open ecosystems. The system also provides multi-dimensional metadata annotation (scene segmentation, motion scoring, OCR ratio, automatic captioning, etc.), laying the foundation for flexible subsequent data `cooking' and indexing\cite{vlogger}.
  This platform aims to significantly lower the barrier to constructing specialized video training datasets through infrastructure-level solutions, while supporting community contributions and a governance-enabled data expansion paradigm. \textbf{Project demo:} https://screenapp.io/app/v/WP0SvffgsH

### [176] [IntSeqBERT: Learning Arithmetic Structure in OEIS via Modulo-Spectrum Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05556)
*Kazuhisa Nakasho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: IntSeqBERT 是一种用于预测 OEIS 整数序列的双流 Transformer 编码器，通过连续对数尺度嵌入和 100 个模数（2-101）的 sin/cos 模嵌入进行融合，采用 FiLM 机制。模型联合训练三个预测头：幅度回归、符号分类和模预测，覆盖 274,705 个序列。在大规模版本（9150 万参数）下，其幅度准确率达到 95.85%，平均模精度（MMA）为 50.38%，分别优于标准令牌化 Transformer 基线 8.9 和 4.5 个百分点。去除模流的消融实验表明，模流贡献了 15.2 个百分点的 MMA 提升，并额外提升幅度准确率 6.2 个百分点。基于概率中国剩余定理（CRT）的求解器将预测结果转化为具体整数，使下一术语预测性能提升 7.4 倍（Top-1：19.09% vs. 2.59%）。模谱分析显示，归一化信息增益（NIG）与欧拉函数比值 φ(m)/m 呈强负相关（r = -0.851，p < 10⁻²⁸），表明复合模数通过 CRT 聚合更高效地捕捉了 OEIS 的算术结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于分词的模型难以处理超出词汇表范围的极大整数值，且无法有效利用整数序列中蕴含的周期性算术结构，导致对 OEIS 序列的预测能力受限。因此，需要一种能够同时建模数值大小和模运算特征的新方法。

Method: IntSeqBERT 采用双流 Transformer 架构，对每个序列元素分别编码：一维为连续的对数尺度幅度嵌入，另一维为 100 个不同模数（2–101）的 sin/cos 模嵌入；两路特征通过 FiLM 机制融合。模型联合训练三个任务：幅度回归、符号分类和模预测。最终使用基于概率 CRT 的求解器将多模预测还原为具体整数。

Result: 在测试集上，大型版 IntSeqBERT 达到 95.85% 的幅度准确率和 50.38% 的平均模精度（MMA），显著优于基线模型（+8.9 和 +4.5 个百分点）。消融实验表明，模流对 MMA 提升贡献达 +15.2 个百分点，并额外提升幅度准确率 +6.2 个百分点。结合 CRT 求解器后，下一术语预测性能提升 7.4 倍（Top-1 从 2.59% 提升至 19.09%）。模谱分析揭示 φ(m)/m 与 NIG 强负相关（r = -0.851，p < 10⁻²⁸），支持复合模数通过 CRT 更高效表达序列结构。

Conclusion: IntSeqBERT 通过引入模数嵌入与对数尺度幅度表示，成功捕捉了 OEIS 序列中的算术结构，尤其在处理大数值和周期性模式方面表现优异。模流的有效性得到实证，而基于 CRT 的求解策略显著提升了实际预测性能。该研究为整数序列建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Integer sequences in the OEIS span values from single-digit constants to astronomical factorials and exponentials, making prediction challenging for standard tokenised models that cannot handle out-of-vocabulary values or exploit periodic arithmetic structure. We present IntSeqBERT, a dual-stream Transformer encoder for masked integer-sequence modelling on OEIS. Each sequence element is encoded along two complementary axes: a continuous log-scale magnitude embedding and sin/cos modulo embeddings for 100 residues (moduli $2$--$101$), fused via FiLM. Three prediction heads (magnitude regression, sign classification, and modulo prediction for 100 moduli) are trained jointly on 274,705 OEIS sequences. At the Large scale (91.5M parameters), IntSeqBERT achieves 95.85% magnitude accuracy and 50.38% Mean Modulo Accuracy (MMA) on the test set, outperforming a standard tokenised Transformer baseline by $+8.9$ pt and $+4.5$ pt, respectively. An ablation removing the modulo stream confirms it accounts for $+15.2$ pt of the MMA gain and contributes an additional $+6.2$ pt to magnitude accuracy. A probabilistic Chinese Remainder Theorem (CRT)-based Solver converts the model's predictions into concrete integers, yielding a 7.4-fold improvement in next-term prediction over the tokenised-Transformer baseline (Top-1: 19.09% vs. 2.59%). Modulo spectrum analysis reveals a strong negative correlation between Normalised Information Gain (NIG) and Euler's totient ratio $\varphi(m)/m$ ($r = -0.851$, $p < 10^{-28}$), providing empirical evidence that composite moduli capture OEIS arithmetic structure more efficiently via CRT aggregation.

</details>


### [177] [Autocorrelation effects in a stochastic-process model for decision making via time series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05559)
*Tomoki Yamagami,Mikio Hasegawa,Takatomo Mihana,Ryoichi Horisaki,Atsushi Uchida*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过一个基于随机过程的模型分析了基于时间序列决策的两臂赌博机问题，发现负自相关在奖励丰富的环境中更优，正自相关在奖励贫乏的环境中更优，当奖励总和为1时性能与自相关无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究光子混沌动力学在多臂赌博机问题中的应用，特别是自相关特性对决策准确性的影 响，但现有实验结果缺乏数学解释，因此需要建立最小数学模型来揭示其内在机制。

Method: 采用基于拔河原理的随机过程模型，结合阈值与二值马尔可夫信号的联合演化，模拟时间序列驱动的决策过程，并通过数值模拟分析不同环境下的最优自相关特性。

Result: 研究发现：在奖励总和大于1的环境中，负自相关表现最佳；在奖励总和小于1的环境中，正自相关更优；当奖励总和等于1时，性能不受自相关影响，这一结论得到数学证明。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了自相关特性在时间序列决策中的环境依赖性作用，为无线通信和机器人强化学习中的决策优化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Decision makers exploiting photonic chaotic dynamics obtained by semiconductor lasers provide an ultrafast approach to solving multi-armed bandit problems by using a temporal optical signal as the driving source for sequential decisions. In such systems, the sampling interval of the chaotic waveform shapes the temporal correlation of the resulting time series, and experiments have reported that decision accuracy depends strongly on this autocorrelation property. However, it remains unclear whether the benefit of autocorrelation can be explained by a minimal mathematical model. Here, we analyze a stochastic-process model of the time-series-based decision making using the tug-of-war principle for solving the two-armed bandit problem, where the threshold and a two-valued Markov signal evolve jointly. Numerical results reveal an environment-dependent structure: negative (positive) autocorrelation is optimal in reward-rich (reward-poor) environments. These findings show that negative autocorrelation of the time series is advantageous when the sum of the winning probabilities is more than $1$, whereas positive autocorrelation is useful when the sum of the winning probabilities is less than $1$. Moreover, the performance is independent of autocorrelation if the sum of the winning probabilities equals $1$, which is mathematically clarified. This study paves the way for improving the decision-making scheme for reinforcement learning applications in wireless communications and robotics.

</details>


### [178] [When AI Levels the Playing Field: Skill Homogenization, Asset Concentration, and Two Regimes of Inequality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05565)
*Xupeng Chen,Shuchen Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨生成式AI如何在缩小个体技能差异的同时，将经济价值向集中化的互补资产转移，导致一个看似矛盾的现象：技术虽使个人表现趋同，却可能加剧总体不平等。研究构建了一个基于任务的模型，包含内生教育、雇主筛选和异质性企业，识别出两种不同制度均衡状态，其边界取决于AI的技术结构（专有型与商品型）及劳动力市场制度（租金共享弹性、资产集中度）。通过模拟矩法校准模型并匹配六个实证目标，敏感性分析表明五个非ΔGini矩仅能识别机制速率，而总体符号由参数m_6和ξ决定；同时，AI技术结构（η₁与η₀）独立地跨越了均衡边界。研究贡献在于揭示机制而非给出不平等方向的结论。使用BLS OEWS数据的职位层面回归显示，现有数据无法检验模型对任务层面的预测，真正的检验需依赖尚未大规模存在的“职位内-任务内”面板数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究生成式AI在提升个体表现一致性的同时，如何通过改变经济价值分配结构，可能加剧总体不平等，揭示其背后的机制与制度条件。

Method: 构建包含内生教育、雇主筛选与异质性企业的任务基础模型，运用方法模拟矩法（Method of Simulated Moments）校准模型，并通过敏感性分解分析关键参数影响，结合实证数据评估模型可测性。

Result: 模型识别出两种均衡状态，其转换边界由AI技术结构与劳动力市场制度共同决定；敏感性分析表明，ΔGini以外的矩仅能识别机制速率，而总体不平等符号由特定参数决定；现有职位层面数据无法验证任务级预测，真正检验需依赖尚未广泛存在的面板数据。

Conclusion: 生成式AI对不平等的影响并非单一方向，而是由技术结构与制度环境共同决定；核心贡献在于提出机制框架，而非预判不平等增减方向，未来需开发更精细的微观面板数据以验证理论预测。

Abstract: Generative AI compresses within-task skill differences while shifting economic value toward concentrated complementary assets, creating an apparent paradox: the technology that equalizes individual performance may widen aggregate inequality. We formalize this tension in a task-based model with endogenous education, employer screening, and heterogeneous firms. The model yields two regimes whose boundary depends on AI's technology structure (proprietary vs.\ commodity) and labor market institutions (rent-sharing elasticity, asset concentration). A scenario analysis via Method of Simulated Moments, matching six empirical targets, disciplines the model's quantitative magnitudes; a sensitivity decomposition reveals that the five non-$Δ$Gini moments identify mechanism rates but not the aggregate sign, which at the calibrated parameters is pinned by $m_6$ and $ξ$, while AI's technology structure ($η_1$ vs.\ $η_0$) independently crosses the boundary. The contribution is the mechanism -- not a verdict on the sign. Occupation-level regressions using BLS OEWS data (2019--2023) illustrate why such data cannot test the model's task-level predictions. The predictions are testable with within-occupation, within-task panel data that do not yet exist at scale.

</details>


### [179] [Aligning the True Semantics: Constrained Decoupling and Distribution Sampling for Cross-Modal Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05566)
*Xiang Ma,Lexin Fang,Litian Xu,Caiming Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CDDS算法，通过约束解耦和分布采样实现跨模态对齐，有效分离语义与模态信息，缓解模态差距带来的偏差，显著提升多模态学习性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法仅关注嵌入一致性，忽略嵌入中的非语义信息，导致语义对齐不准确；现有解耦方法缺乏明确区分语义与模态信息的标准，且模态差异易引发对齐偏差或信息丢失。

Method: 引入双路径UNet进行自适应嵌入解耦，并施加多重约束以确保有效分离；设计分布采样方法以弥合模态差距，提升对齐合理性。

Result: 在多个基准数据集和模型架构上实验验证，CDDS显著优于现有最先进方法，性能提升达6.6%至14.2%。

Conclusion: CDDS通过约束解耦与分布采样有效实现了跨模态语义对齐，解决了现有方法中语义与模态信息混淆及模态差距问题，具有显著的性能优势。

Abstract: Cross-modal alignment is a crucial task in multimodal learning aimed at achieving semantic consistency between vision and language. This requires that image-text pairs exhibit similar semantics. Traditional algorithms pursue embedding consistency to achieve semantic consistency, ignoring the non-semantic information present in the embedding. An intuitive approach is to decouple the embeddings into semantic and modality components, aligning only the semantic component. However, this introduces two main challenges: (1) There is no established standard for distinguishing semantic and modal information. (2) The modality gap can cause semantic alignment deviation or information loss. To align the true semantics, we propose a novel cross-modal alignment algorithm via \textbf{C}onstrained \textbf{D}ecoupling and \textbf{D}istribution \textbf{S}ampling (CDDS). Specifically, (1) A dual-path UNet is introduced to adaptively decouple the embeddings, applying multiple constraints to ensure effective separation. (2) A distribution sampling method is proposed to bridge the modality gap, ensuring the rationality of the alignment process. Extensive experiments on various benchmarks and model backbones demonstrate the superiority of CDDS, outperforming state-of-the-art methods by 6.6\% to 14.2\%.

</details>


### [180] [FuseDiff: Symmetry-Preserving Joint Diffusion for Dual-Target Structure-Based Drug Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05567)
*Jianliang Wu,Anjie Qiao,Zhen Wang,Zhewei Wei,Sheng Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FuseDiff is an end-to-end diffusion model for dual-target structure-based drug design that jointly generates a ligand and two target-specific binding poses. It uses a message-passing backbone with Dual-target Local Context Fusion (DLCF) to integrate local context from both pockets, preserving symmetry while enabling geometric adaptation. Explicit bond generation ensures topological consistency across poses. The method achieves state-of-the-art docking performance and enables systematic pose quality assessment prior to docking.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing dual-target drug design methods use staged pipelines with either unrealistic independence assumptions or overly rigid correlations, failing to jointly generate two target-specific binding poses. There is a need for a unified, expressive model that can simultaneously generate ligands and compatible poses for two targets.

Method: FuseDiff employs a diffusion model with a message-passing backbone featuring Dual-target Local Context Fusion (DLCF), which fuses local atomic contexts from both target pockets. It jointly generates the molecular graph and two binding poses, enforcing topological consistency via explicit bond generation while allowing target-specific geometric adjustments.

Result: FuseDiff outperforms existing methods in docking accuracy on benchmark and real-world dual-target systems. It enables the first systematic evaluation of dual-target pose quality before docking-based search, demonstrating superior joint modeling of ligand and multiple binding modes.

Conclusion: FuseDiff provides a powerful, end-to-end solution for dual-target drug design by jointly generating ligands and target-specific poses with improved expressiveness and consistency, paving the way for more effective polypharmacological therapies.

Abstract: Dual-target structure-based drug design aims to generate a single ligand together with two pocket-specific binding poses, each compatible with a corresponding target pocket, enabling polypharmacological therapies with improved efficacy and reduced resistance. Existing approaches typically rely on staged pipelines, which either decouple the two poses via conditional-independence assumptions or enforce overly rigid correlations, and therefore fail to jointly generate two target-specific binding modes. To address this, we propose FuseDiff, an end-to-end diffusion model that jointly generates a ligand molecular graph and two pocket-specific binding poses conditioned on both pockets. FuseDiff features a message-passing backbone with Dual-target Local Context Fusion (DLCF), which fuses each ligand atom's local context from both pockets to enable expressive joint modeling while preserving the desired symmetries. Together with explicit bond generation, FuseDiff enforces topological consistency across the two poses under a shared graph while allowing target-specific geometric adaptation in each pocket. To support principled training and evaluation, we derive a dual-target training set and use an independent held-out test set for evaluation. Experiments on the benchmark and a real-world dual-target system show that FuseDiff achieves state-of-the-art docking performance and enables the first systematic assessment of dual-target pose quality prior to docking-based pose search.

</details>

Our theory formulates a correspondence between the depth of a sequence model and the tower of Lie algebra extensions. Echoing recent theoretical studies, we characterize the Lie-algebraic class of constant-depth sequence models and their corresponding expressivity bounds. Abstract: Railcar shunting is a core planning task in freight railyards, where yard planners need to disassemble and reassemble groups of railcars to form outbound trains. Classification tracks with access from one side only can be considered as stack structures, where railcars are added and removed from only one end, leading to a last-in-first-out (LIFO) retrieval order. In contrast, two-sided tracks function like queue structures, allowing railcars to be added from one end and removed from the opposite end, following a first-in-first-out (FIFO) order. We consider a problem requiring assembly of multiple outbound trains using two locomotives in a railyard with two-sided classification track access. To address this combinatorially challenging problem class, we decompose the problem into two subproblems, each with one-sided classification track access and a locomotive on each side. We present a novel Hybrid Heuristic-Reinforcement Learning (HHRL) framework that integrates railway-specific heuristic solution approaches with a reinforcement learning method, specifically Q-learning. The proposed framework leverages methods to decrease the state-action space and guide exploration during reinforcement learning. The results of a series of numerical experiments demonstrate the efficiency and quality of the HHRL algorithm in both one-sided access, single-locomotive problems and two-sided access, two-locomotive problems.

### [183] [On the Value of Tokeniser Pretraining in Physics Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05598)

Method: 采用自编码目标对分词器进行预训练，随后训练动力学模型；结合灵活的时空压缩操作（扩展因果卷积），支持运行时可调压缩比，以适应不同下游任务。

Modern high-resolution simulations produce vast volumes of data spanning diverse physical regimes and scales. Training foundation models to learn the dynamics underlying such data enables the modelling of complex multiphysics phenomena, especially in data-limited settings. The emerging class of physics foundation models typically aims to learn two tasks jointly: (i) extracting compact representations of high-resolution spatiotemporal data, and (ii) capturing governing physical dynamics. However, learning both tasks from scratch simultaneously can impede the effectiveness of either process. We demonstrate that pretraining the tokeniser with an autoencoding objective prior to training the dynamics model enhances computational efficiency for downstream tasks. Notably, the magnitude of this benefit depends on domain alignment: pretraining on the same physical system as the downstream task yields the largest improvements, while pretraining on other systems provides moderate gains. In-domain pretraining reduces VRMSE by 64% after 10,500 training steps compared to training from scratch. To our knowledge, this is the first systematic investigation of tokeniser pretraining for physics foundation models. We further introduce flexible spatiotemporal compression operations that extend causal convolutions to support runtime-adjustable compression ratios, enabling efficient adaptation to diverse downstream tasks. Our findings provide practical guidance for training efficient physics emulators and highlight the importance of strategic pretraining data selection.

In this paper we consider a different task for defending the adversary, focusing on the attacker, rather than the attack. We present and demonstrate a framework for identifying characteristics about the attacker from an observed attack.
  We prove that, without additional knowledge, the attacker is non-identifiable (multiple potential attackers would perform the same observed attack). To address this challenge, we propose a domain-agnostic framework to identify the most probable attacker. This framework aids the defender in two ways. First, knowledge about the attacker can be leveraged for exogenous mitigation (i.e., addressing the vulnerability by altering the decision-making system outside the learning algorithm and/or limiting the attacker's capability). Second, when implementing defense methods that directly affect the learning process (e.g., adversarial regularization), knowledge of the specific attacker improves performance. We present the details of our framework and illustrate its applicability through specific instantiations on a variety of learners.

Abstract: It is increasingly common in machine learning to use learned models to label data and then employ such data to train more capable models. The phenomenon of weak-to-strong generalization exemplifies the advantage of this two-stage procedure: a strong student is trained on imperfect labels obtained from a weak teacher, and yet the strong student outperforms the weak teacher. In this paper, we show that the potential improvement is substantial, in the sense that it affects the scaling law followed by the test error. Specifically, we consider students and teachers trained via random feature ridge regression (RFRR). Our main technical contribution is to derive a deterministic equivalent for the excess test error of the student trained on labels obtained via the teacher. Via this deterministic equivalent, we then identify regimes in which the scaling law of the student improves upon that of the teacher, unveiling that the improvement can be achieved both in bias-dominated and variance-dominated settings. Strikingly, the student may attain the minimax optimal rate regardless of the scaling law of the teacher -- in fact, when the test error of the teacher does not even decay with the sample size.

### [187] [Revisiting the (Sub)Optimality of Best-of-N for Inference-Time Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05739)
*Ved Sriraman,Adam Block*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Best-of-N (BoN) sampling is a popular inference-time alignment method for language models, where N responses are sampled and the highest-scoring one according to a reward model is selected. While previous theoretical work criticized BoN for being statistically suboptimal and prone to reward hacking, this paper re-evaluates BoN under more practical assumptions. Instead of focusing on expected true reward, it analyzes win-rate—a pairwise comparison metric aligned with how reward models are trained and evaluated. The authors show that properly tuned BoN is both computationally and statistically optimal for maximizing win-rate, explaining its practical success. They also propose a modified BoN variant that eliminates reward-hacking while preserving optimal performance. Finally, they demonstrate that prior methods are provably suboptimal when considering win-rate, underscoring the importance of aligning analysis objectives with real-world evaluation practices.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To better understand why Best-of-N (BoN) sampling works well in practice despite theoretical concerns about statistical suboptimality and reward hacking. Previous analyses focused on expected true reward, which may not reflect real-world training and evaluation settings. This study shifts focus to win-rate, a more relevant metric tied to how reward models are actually trained and assessed.

Method: The paper conducts a theoretical analysis of BoN under realistic assumptions regarding reference and reward models. It evaluates performance using win-rate as the primary objective, rather than expected true reward. The authors derive conditions under which BoN is statistically and computationally optimal for win-rate maximization. They further propose a modified BoN variant designed to eliminate reward-hacking while maintaining optimal statistical performance. Theoretical proofs are provided to support claims of optimality and robustness.

Result: Properly tuned Best-of-N (BoN) is shown to be both computationally and statistically optimal for maximizing win-rate under minimal assumptions on model quality. A proposed variant of BoN successfully eliminates reward-hacking without sacrificing statistical efficiency. Prior approaches are proven to be suboptimal when evaluated based on win-rate, highlighting the need for appropriate objective alignment in theoretical analysis.

Conclusion: Best-of-N sampling remains a highly effective inference-time alignment method when evaluated through the lens of win-rate, a practically relevant metric. Its success can be theoretically justified under realistic assumptions. The proposed modification provides a robust solution to reward-hacking while preserving optimality. These findings emphasize that the choice of evaluation objective significantly impacts the assessment of alignment methods.

Abstract: Best-of-N (BoN) sampling is a widely used inference-time alignment method for language models, whereby N candidate responses are sampled from a reference model and the one with the highest predicted reward according to a learned reward model is selected. Despite its widespread practical use, recent theoretical work has suggested that it is statistically suboptimal and vulnerable to reward hacking, the process by which models exploit weaknesses in the learned reward model to achieve high estimated reward without genuinely improving performance. We revisit this question under assumptions that more closely reflect practice than that of prior work. In particular, in contradistinction to earlier analyses that focused on expected true reward, which may not be meaningful in many practical settings, we investigate how inference-time alignment affects the win-rate, a pairwise comparison-based metric more closely aligned with how reward models are trained and evaluated in practice. We demonstrate that, under minimal conditions on the quality of the reference model and learned reward model, properly tuned BoN is both computationally and statistically optimal in achieving high win-rate, partially explaining its widespread practical success. Because BoN remains susceptible to reward-hacking in this setting, we propose a simple and practical variant that provably eliminates reward-hacking while maintaining optimal statistical performance. Finally, we show that prior approaches are provably suboptimal when considering win-rate, highlighting the importance of choosing appropriate objectives when analyzing inference-time alignment methods.

### [188] [MIRACL: A Diverse Meta-Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Objective Multi-Echelon Combinatorial Supply Chain Optimisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05760)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多目标强化学习（MORL）在动态环境中部署受限于任务特定的重新训练需求和高昂的计算成本，亟需一种能够快速适应新任务且高效通用的方法。

Method: MIRACL 采用分层元学习架构，将每个任务分解为结构化子问题，利用基于帕累托的适应策略在跨任务间元学习全局策略，以增强多样性并支持高效政策适应。

Result: 在供应链优化场景下的实证评估显示，MIRACL 在简单至中等复杂度任务中表现优异，相比传统 MORL 基线，最大提升达 10% 的超体积和 5% 的期望效用。

Conclusion: MIRACL 为多目标决策问题提供了一种高效、鲁棒的少样本适应机制，具有理论上的领域无关性，可广泛应用于各类动态多目标决策场景。

Abstract: Multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL) is effective for multi-echelon combinatorial supply chain optimisation, where tasks involve high dimensionality, uncertainty, and competing objectives. However, its deployment in dynamic environments is hindered by the need for task-specific retraining and substantial computational cost. We introduce MIRACL (Meta multI-objective Reinforcement leArning with Composite Learning), a hierarchical Meta-MORL framework that allows for a few-shot generalisation across diverse tasks. MIRACL decomposes each task into structured subproblems for efficient policy adaptation and meta-learns a global policy across tasks using a Pareto-based adaptation strategy to encourage diversity in meta-training and fine-tuning. To our knowledge, this is the first integration of Meta-MORL with such mechanisms in combinatorial optimisation. Although validated in the supply chain domain, MIRACL is theoretically domain-agnostic and applicable to broader dynamic multi-objective decision-making problems. Empirical evaluations show that MIRACL outperforms conventional MORL baselines in simple to moderate tasks, achieving up to 10% higher hypervolume and 5% better expected utility. These results underscore the potential of MIRACL for robust, efficient adaptation in multi-objective problems.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在控制Rectified Flow模型进行精确任务（如语义编辑或盲图像恢复）时面临挑战，包括基于反演的引导存在几何锁定问题，而后验采样近似方法计算成本高且不稳定。

Method: 将恢复任务重新表述为一个近端优化问题，构建结合输入保真度与预训练得分场真实性的能量景观，并证明该目标具有正常收缩性质，确保分布外输入被拉回数据流形上，有效逼近流形上的后验模态。

Result: SGPP在无需训练的情况下实现了对生成自由度与身份保持之间连续可控的权衡，能泛化现有最先进的编辑方法，例如RF反演是其极限情况；同时在稳定性和效率上优于传统方法。

Conclusion: SGPP提供了一种统一、高效且灵活的框架，用于控制Rectified Flow模型完成精确生成任务，兼具理论保障与实际性能优势。

Abstract: Rectified Flow (RF) models achieve state-of-the-art generation quality, yet controlling them for precise tasks -- such as semantic editing or blind image recovery -- remains a challenge. Current approaches bifurcate into inversion-based guidance, which suffers from "geometric locking" by rigidly adhering to the source trajectory, and posterior sampling approximations (e.g., DPS), which are computationally expensive and unstable. In this work, we propose Score-Guided Proximal Projection (SGPP), a unified framework that bridges the gap between deterministic optimization and stochastic sampling. We reformulate the recovery task as a proximal optimization problem, defining an energy landscape that balances fidelity to the input with realism from the pre-trained score field. We theoretically prove that this objective induces a normal contraction property, geometrically guaranteeing that out-of-distribution inputs are snapped onto the data manifold, and it effectively reaches the posterior mode constrained to the manifold. Crucially, we demonstrate that SGPP generalizes state-of-the-art editing methods: RF-inversion is effectively a limiting case of our framework. By relaxing the proximal variance, SGPP enables "soft guidance," offering a continuous, training-free trade-off between strict identity preservation and generative freedom.

### [190] [Bridging Domains through Subspace-Aware Model Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05768)
*Levy Chaves,Chao Zhou,Rebekka Burkholz,Eduardo Valle,Sandra Avila*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究模型合并中领域泛化问题，发现不同领域微调模型合并时会产生更强的参数冲突。为此提出SCORE方法，通过共享正交基和投影修剪来缓解子空间冲突，在多种架构和规模下均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型合并方法在领域泛化方面研究不足，尤其在不同分布偏移下的模型合并存在严重参数冲突，亟需有效解决方案。

Method: 提出SCORE方法，通过奇异值分解计算所有模型主奇异向量的拼接主成分，构建共享正交基，并将各任务矩阵投影至该基上，剪除非对角线成分以消除冲突方向。

Result: SCORE在多个架构和模型规模下显著优于现有合并方法，在领域泛化任务中表现出更强性能与可扩展性。

Conclusion: SCORE有效缓解了跨领域模型合并中的子空间冲突，显著提升模型在未见领域的泛化能力，具有良好的通用性和实用性。

Abstract: Model merging integrates multiple task-specific models into a single consolidated one. Recent research has made progress in improving merging performance for in-distribution or multi-task scenarios, but domain generalization in model merging remains underexplored. We investigate how merging models fine-tuned on distinct domains affects generalization to unseen domains. Through an analysis of parameter competition in the task matrix using singular value decomposition, we show that merging models trained under different distribution shifts induces stronger conflicts between their subspaces compared to traditional multi-task settings. To mitigate this issue, we propose SCORE (Subspace COnflict-Resolving mErging), a method designed to alleviate such singular subspace conflicts. SCORE finds a shared orthogonal basis by computing the principal components of the concatenated leading singular vectors of all models. It then projects each task matrix into the shared basis, pruning off-diagonal components to remove conflicting singular directions. SCORE consistently outperforms, on average, existing model merging approaches in domain generalization settings across a variety of architectures and model scales, demonstrating its effectiveness and scalability.

### [191] [First-Order Softmax Weighted Switching Gradient Method for Distributed Stochastic Minimax Optimization with Stochastic Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05774)
*Zhankun Luo,Antesh Upadhyay,Sang Bin Moon,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于联邦学习的新型一阶Softmax加权切换梯度方法，用于解决分布式随机极小极大优化问题。在全客户端参与下，算法达到标准$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$的查询复杂度，满足最优性间隙与可行性容差统一为$ε$的界；在部分参与的实际场景中，通过随机优势假设量化客户端采样噪声。通过放松目标函数的有界性假设，建立了更紧的Softmax超参数下界，并提供统一的误差分解和$\mathcal{O}(\log\frac{1}{δ})$高概率收敛保证。实验验证了该方法在Neyman-Pearson分类与公平分类任务中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于原始-对偶或惩罚的方法存在超参数敏感性和收敛振荡问题，难以稳定优化最坏情况下的客户端性能。因此需要一种更稳健、无需复杂双循环结构的优化机制，以适应联邦学习中客户端异构与部分参与的现实挑战。

Method: 提出一种单循环仅优化主变量的切换梯度方法，结合Softmax加权策略实现客户端间权重动态调整；引入随机优势假设建模客户端采样噪声；采用统一误差分解分析框架，推导高概率收敛结果。

Result: 在全参与情况下，实现$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$的查询复杂度；在部分参与下，获得$\mathcal{O}(\log\frac{1}{δ})$高概率收敛率；相比传统方法，显著降低超参数敏感性，提升稳定性；实验表明在NP分类与公平分类任务中具有优越性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的Softmax-Weighted Switching Gradient方法为分布式极小极大优化提供了高效稳定的解决方案，尤其适用于联邦学习中客户端异构和不完全参与的场景，其单循环设计有效规避了传统方法的缺陷，具备良好的理论保障与实际应用价值。

Abstract: This paper addresses the distributed stochastic minimax optimization problem subject to stochastic constraints. We propose a novel first-order Softmax-Weighted Switching Gradient method tailored for federated learning. Under full client participation, our algorithm achieves the standard $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$ oracle complexity to satisfy a unified bound $ε$ for both the optimality gap and feasibility tolerance. We extend our theoretical analysis to the practical partial participation regime by quantifying client sampling noise through a stochastic superiority assumption. Furthermore, by relaxing standard boundedness assumptions on the objective functions, we establish a strictly tighter lower bound for the softmax hyperparameter. We provide a unified error decomposition and establish a sharp $\mathcal{O}(\log\frac{1}δ)$ high-probability convergence guarantee. Ultimately, our framework demonstrates that a single-loop primal-only switching mechanism provides a stable alternative for optimizing worst-case client performance, effectively bypassing the hyperparameter sensitivity and convergence oscillations often encountered in traditional primal-dual or penalty-based approaches. We verify the efficacy of our algorithm via experiment on the Neyman-Pearson (NP) classification and fair classification tasks.

### [193] [MoE Lens -- An Expert Is All You Need](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05806)
*Marmik Chaudhari,Idhant Gulati,Nishkal Hundia,Pranav Karra,Shivam Raval*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究系统分析了Mixture of Experts (MoE)模型中专家的专业化行为，发现尽管有64个专家且每层激活6个，但模型主要依赖少数几个专业化专家。顶层专家的输出几乎可近似全集成预测结果，且少量专家处理超过50%的路由决策。各层单个专家与集成专家的隐藏状态相似度极高（最高达0.95），使用单一专家仅导致困惑度上升5%，表明专家能力高度集中。该发现为通过针对性剪枝优化推理效率提供了可能，并揭示了知识在模型中的局部化特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE模型虽可通过稀疏激活实现参数高效扩展，但其推理和内存开销仍难以优化，主要原因在于对专家专业化行为理解不足。亟需深入分析专家如何分工与贡献，以探索优化路径。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：一是分析领域特定的路由模式；二是提出早期解码框架，追踪专家对输出表示的贡献。结合对DeepSeekMoE模型的实证分析，量化评估专家路由分布、隐藏状态相似性及性能退化情况。

Result: 结果显示，极少数专家承担主要任务，顶层专家输出可近似全集成预测；部分层中单个专家与集成专家的隐藏状态相似度高达0.95，仅造成5%的困惑度上升；多数路由决策由少数专家完成，表明专家能力高度集中。

Conclusion: MoE模型表现出显著的知识集中化现象，即少数专家掌握核心能力，这为通过选择性剪枝降低推理成本提供了可行路径，同时为研究模型内部知识定位机制开辟新方向。

Abstract: Mixture of Experts (MoE) models enable parameter-efficient scaling through sparse expert activations, yet optimizing their inference and memory costs remains challenging due to limited understanding of their specialization behavior. We present a systematic analysis of expert specialization in MoEs through two complementary approaches: domain-specific routing patterns and an early decoding framework that tracks expert contributions to output representations. Our analysis of the DeepSeekMoE model reveals that despite having 64 routed experts with 6 active for each layer's computation, the model predominantly relies on a few specialized experts, with the top-weighted expert's output closely approximating the full ensemble prediction. We quantitatively validate these findings through a systematic analysis of the token routing distribution, demonstrating that very few experts handle over 50\% of routing decisions across different specialized domains. Hidden state similarity between single and ensemble experts for every layer is extremely high, with some layers having cosine similarity as high as 0.95 and perplexity increasing by only 5\% when using a single expert across all three domains. Our results indicate that Mixture of Experts models exhibit concentrated expertise highlighting potential opportunities for inference optimization through targeted expert pruning while maintaining model performance and opening avenues towards studying localization of learned knowledge in these models.

### [194] [Self-Auditing Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning for Few-Shot 3D Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05822)
*Son Thai Ly,Hien V. Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SEA-PEFT 是一种自审计的参数高效微调方法，旨在自动化临床领域中基础模型的适配过程。针对域偏移和标注数据稀缺的问题，该方法将适配器配置视为在线分配问题，在微调过程中通过搜索-审计-分配循环动态选择最优适配器组合。利用指数移动平均与四分位距平滑技术，并结合有限状态排名控制器，提升在高噪声少样本场景下的稳定性。实验表明，SEA-PEFT 在 1/5/10-shot 设置下相比最强固定拓扑基线提升 2.4–2.8 点 Dice 分数，且仅训练不到 1% 的参数。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床场景中基础模型的适配面临域偏移和标注数据稀缺的挑战，而现有参数高效微调（PEFT）方法要么需要人工配置适配器结构，要么依赖计算成本高昂的自动化搜索，在少样本3D医学图像分割任务中难以应用。缺乏专业AI工程师支持导致适应周期长，亟需自动化、高效的解决方案。

Method: SEA-PEFT 将适配器配置建模为在线分配问题，采用搜索-审计-分配循环：在训练中激活部分适配器，通过临时关闭每个适配器并评估其对性能的影响（Dice utility），再基于参数预算使用贪心背包算法重新选择活跃适配器集；引入指数移动平均与四分位距平滑以降低噪声影响，结合有限状态排名控制器增强系统稳定性。

Result: 在 TotalSegmentator 和 FLARE'22 数据集上，SEA-PEFT 在 1/5/10-shot 设置下均优于最强的固定拓扑 PEFT 基线，平均 Dice 提升 2.4–2.8 点，同时仅训练不到 1% 的参数，显著提升效率与实用性。

Conclusion: SEA-PEFT 实现了无需人工干预的自动化适配，有效应对少样本、高噪声的临床医学图像分割挑战，具备良好的可扩展性与实际部署潜力，为资源受限的医疗团队提供了一种高效、可靠的模型迁移方案。

Abstract: Adapting foundation models to new clinical sites remains challenging in practice. Domain shift and scarce annotations must be handled by experts, yet many clinical groups do not have ready access to skilled AI engineers to tune adapter designs and training recipes. As a result, adaptation cycles can stretch from weeks to months, particularly in few-shot settings. Existing PEFT methods either require manual adapter configuration or automated searches that are computationally infeasible in few-shot 3D settings. We propose SEA-PEFT (SElf-Auditing Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning) to automate this process. SEA-PEFT treats adapter configuration as an online allocation problem solved during fine-tuning rather than through manual, fixed-topology choices. SEA-PEFT uses a search-audit-allocate loop that trains active adapters, estimates each adapter's Dice utility by momentarily toggling it off, and then reselects the active set under a parameter budget using a greedy knapsack allocator. Exponential Moving Average and Interquartile Range smoothing, together with a Finite-State Ranking controller, stabilize the loop and improve reliability in high-noise few-shot regimes. On TotalSegmentator and FLARE'22, SEA-PEFT improves mean Dice by 2.4--2.8 points over the strongest fixed-topology PEFT baselines across 1/5/10-shot settings while training <1% of parameters. For reproducibility purposes, we made our code publicly available at https://github.com/tsly123/SEA_PEFT

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解多示例提示在测试时适应中的可靠性与边界，尤其针对开源大语言模型，以优化其在实际应用中的有效性。

Method: 采用实证方法，系统评估多示例提示在多种任务和模型上的表现，分析更新幅度、示例顺序及选择策略的影响；同时比较动态与强化ICL等替代策略。

Result: 多示例提示在结构化任务中表现良好，信息增益高；但在开放式生成任务中效果有限，且高度依赖示例选择策略。动态和强化ICL能更有效地控制信息注入，提升适应性。

Abstract: Test-time adaptation enables large language models (LLMs) to modify their behavior at inference without updating model parameters. A common approach is many-shot prompting, where large numbers of in-context learning (ICL) examples are injected as an input-space test-time update. Although performance can improve as more demonstrations are added, the reliability and limits of this update mechanism remain poorly understood, particularly for open-source models. We present an empirical study of many-shot prompting across tasks and model backbones, analyzing how performance varies with update magnitude, example ordering, and selection policy. We further study Dynamic and Reinforced ICL as alternative test-time update strategies that control which information is injected and how it constrains model behavior. We find that many-shot prompting is effective for structured tasks where demonstrations provide high information gain, but is highly sensitive to selection strategy and often shows limited benefits for open-ended generation tasks. Overall, we characterize the practical limits of prompt-based test-time adaptation and outline when input-space updates are beneficial versus harmful.

### [196] [Reference-guided Policy Optimization for Molecular Optimization via LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05900)
*Xuan Li,Zhanke Zhou,Zongze Li,Jiangchao Yao,Yu Rong,Lu Zhang,Bo Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RePO是一种在无需轨迹数据的情况下，从参考分子学习的优化方法，通过结合强化学习以促进探索，同时利用参考引导来缓解奖励稀疏性并稳定训练，显著提升分子优化任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基于指令的分子优化任务中，传统的监督微调（SFT）和基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）表现不佳，主要因为缺乏逐步优化轨迹数据，且奖励稀疏、模型探索能力弱，导致学习效率低。

Method: RePO通过在每次更新时从模型采样候选分子及其中间推理轨迹，使用衡量属性满足度与相似性约束的可验证奖励进行强化学习训练；同时引入参考引导机制，将中间推理轨迹作为上下文，仅对答案部分进行监督训练，从而平衡探索与利用。

Result: 在多个分子优化基准测试中，RePO均显著优于SFT和RLVR基线（如GRPO），在优化指标（成功率×相似性）上取得提升，更好地平衡多目标，并展现出更强的未见指令风格泛化能力。

Conclusion: RePO有效解决了分子优化中因缺乏轨迹数据和奖励稀疏性带来的挑战，通过结合探索性强化学习与参考引导的监督学习，实现了更高效、稳定且泛化能力强的分子设计优化。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) benefit substantially from supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) in reasoning tasks. However, these recipes perform poorly in instruction-based molecular optimization, where each data point typically provides only a single optimized reference molecule and no step-by-step optimization trajectory. We reveal that answer-only SFT on the reference molecules collapses reasoning, and RLVR provides sparse feedback under similarity constraints due to the model's lack of effective exploration, which slows learning and limits optimization. To encourage the exploration of new molecules while balancing the exploitation of the reference molecules, we introduce Reference-guided Policy Optimization (RePO), an optimization approach that learns from reference molecules without requiring trajectory data. At each update, RePO samples candidate molecules with their intermediate reasoning trajectories from the model and trains the model using verifiable rewards that measure property satisfaction under similarity constraints in an RL manner. Meanwhile, it applies reference guidance by keeping the policy's intermediate reasoning trajectory as context and training only the answer in a supervised manner. Together, the RL term promotes exploration, while the guidance term mitigates reward sparsity and stabilizes training by grounding outputs to references when many valid molecular edits exist. Across molecular optimization benchmarks, RePO consistently outperforms SFT and RLVR baselines (e.g., GRPO), achieving improvements on the optimization metric (Success Rate $\times$ Similarity), improving balance across competing objectives, and generalizing better to unseen instruction styles. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/tmlr-group/RePO.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多臂赌博机算法（如UCB、Thompson Sampling）的在线实验因依赖历史交互而难以进行可靠推断，需要大量独立重启，导致实验成本高、部署延迟。现有方法在比较不同策略时效率低下，亟需更高效的实验设计。

Method: 提出Artificial Replay（AR）设计：先运行一个策略并记录其轨迹；当测试第二个策略时，若其选择的动作曾在第一个策略中出现过，则重用已记录的奖励，否则才向真实环境查询。建立新的分析框架以证明该方法的统计性质。

Result: AR估计器是无偏的，所需用户交互数约为$T + o(T)$，远低于传统方法的$2T$，显著降低实验成本；方差随$T$次线性增长，优于传统方法的线性增长，提升估计稳定性。数值实验验证了对UCB、Thompson Sampling和ε-greedy等策略的有效性。

Conclusion: Artificial Replay是一种高效、低代价的多臂赌博机算法比较新方法，兼具无偏性、低交互成本和低方差，适用于实际在线平台的快速决策与部署。

Abstract: Online platforms routinely compare multi-armed bandit algorithms, such as UCB and Thompson Sampling, to select the best-performing policy. Unlike standard A/B tests for static treatments, each run of a bandit algorithm over $T$ users produces only one dependent trajectory, because the algorithm's decisions depend on all past interactions. Reliable inference therefore demands many independent restarts of the algorithm, making experimentation costly and delaying deployment decisions. We propose Artificial Replay (AR) as a new experimental design for this problem. AR first runs one policy and records its trajectory. When the second policy is executed, it reuses a recorded reward whenever it selects an action the first policy already took, and queries the real environment only otherwise. We develop a new analytical framework for this design and prove three key properties of the resulting estimator: it is unbiased; it requires only $T + o(T)$ user interactions instead of $2T$ for a run of the treatment and control policies, nearly halving the experimental cost when both policies have sub-linear regret; and its variance grows sub-linearly in $T$, whereas the estimator from a naïve design has a linearly-growing variance. Numerical experiments with UCB, Thompson Sampling, and $ε$-greedy policies confirm these theoretical gains.

</details>

Method: 提出OMGD方法，通过掩码遍历机制实现内存高效优化，并结合非凸分析推导出更优的收敛复杂度。

Result: OMGD在理论和实验上均表现优越：理论复杂度为$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-3})$，且在实际任务中显著优于基准方法。

We propose Omni-Masked Gradient Descent (OMGD), an optimization method based on mask traversal for memory efficient training, and provide a nonconvex convergence analysis that establishes a strictly improved iteration complexity of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-3})$ for finding an $ε$-approximate stationary point. Empirically, OMGD is a lightweight, plug-and-play approach that integrates seamlessly into most mainstream optimizers, yielding consistent improvements over competitive baselines in both fine-tuning and pre-training tasks.

### [199] [Preventing Learning Stagnation in PPO by Scaling to 1 Million Parallel Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06009)
*Michael Beukman,Khimya Khetarpal,Zeyu Zheng,Will Dabney,Jakob Foerster,Michael Dennis,Clare Lyle*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究深度强化学习中PPO算法在某些场景下出现的性能停滞（plateau）问题，发现其根源并非传统探索、容量或优化挑战，而是样本估计的损失逐渐偏离真实目标。通过将PPO外层循环建模为随机优化过程，提出步长过大与噪声过高会导致性能停滞。解决方法包括减小步长或增加采样数量。实验验证模型预测，并表明增加并行环境数是有效手段；同时提出协同调整超参数的策略，错误调整可能导致严重性能下降。最终在复杂开放域中，通过将PPO扩展至超过100万并行环境，实现单调提升，达到一万亿步训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PPO在某些情况下会出现性能停滞，但现有解释（如探索不足、容量限制、优化困难）无法充分说明该现象。需要从新的视角理解其根本原因。

Method: 将PPO外层循环建模为随机优化过程，分析步长与梯度噪声的关系，推导出导致性能停滞的条件，并通过实验验证模型预测。同时提出并行化时的超参数协同调整策略。

Result: 通过增加并行环境数量并合理调整超参数，成功避免性能停滞，在复杂任务中实现单调性能提升，训练规模达一万亿步，显著超越先前基线。

Conclusion: PPO中的性能停滞主要源于样本估计偏差与优化步长/噪声失衡，通过增加并行环境数和正确协同调整超参数，可有效克服该问题，实现高效、稳定的训练。

Abstract: Plateaus, where an agent's performance stagnates at a suboptimal level, are a common problem in deep on-policy RL. Focusing on PPO due to its widespread adoption, we show that plateaus in certain regimes arise not because of known exploration, capacity, or optimization challenges, but because sample-based estimates of the loss eventually become poor proxies for the true objective over the course of training. As a recap, PPO switches between sampling rollouts from several parallel environments online using the current policy (which we call the outer loop) and performing repeated minibatch SGD steps against this offline dataset (the inner loop). In our work we consider only the outer loop, and conceptually model it as stochastic optimization. The step size is then controlled by the regularization strength towards the previous policy and the gradient noise by the number of samples collected between policy update steps. This model predicts that performance will plateau at a suboptimal level if the outer step size is too large relative to the noise. Recasting PPO in this light makes it clear that there are two ways to address this particular type of learning stagnation: either reduce the step size or increase the number of samples collected between updates. We first validate the predictions of our model and investigate how hyperparameter choices influence the step size and update noise, concluding that increasing the number of parallel environments is a simple and robust way to reduce both factors. Next, we propose a recipe for how to co-scale the other hyperparameters when increasing parallelization, and show that incorrectly doing so can lead to severe performance degradation. Finally, we vastly outperform prior baselines in a complex open-ended domain by scaling PPO to more than 1M parallel environments, thereby enabling monotonic performance improvement up to one trillion transitions.

</details>

Abstract: The complexity of learning a concept class under Gaussian marginals in the difficult agnostic model is closely related to its $L_1$-approximability by low-degree polynomials. For any concept class with Gaussian surface area at most $Γ$, Klivans et al. (2008) show that degree $d = O(Γ^2 / \varepsilon^4)$ suffices to achieve an $\varepsilon$-approximation. This leads to the best-known bounds on the complexity of learning a variety of concept classes. In this note, we improve their analysis by showing that degree $d = \tilde O (Γ^2 / \varepsilon^2)$ is enough. In light of lower bounds due to Diakonikolas et al. (2021), this yields (near) optimal bounds on the complexity of agnostically learning polynomial threshold functions in the statistical query model. Our proof relies on a direct analogue of a construction of Feldman et al. (2020), who considered $L_1$-approximation on the Boolean hypercube.
